//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/46px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>Palestine: President <a href="/wiki/Mahmoud_Abbas" title="Mahmoud Abbas">Mahmoud Abbas</a> said in a statement that "Palestine was \xe2\x80\x93 and shall remain \xe2\x80\x93 on the side of Saudi Arabia."<sup id="cite_ref-middleeasteye_136-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-middleeasteye-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Flag_of_the_United_Arab_Emirates.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_Arab_Emirates.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Flag_of_the_United_Arab_Emirates.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_Arab_Emirates.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Flag_of_the_United_Arab_Emirates.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_Arab_Emirates.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>United Arab Emirates: Minister of State for Foreign Affairs <a href="/wiki/Anwar_Gargash" title="Anwar Gargash">Anwar Gargash</a> advised against destabilizing and politically targeting Saudi Arabia and tweeted "the repercussions of the political targeting of Saudi Arabia will be dire for those who fuel it. It remains that the success of Saudi Arabia is what the region and its people want."<sup id="cite_ref-middleeasteye_136-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-middleeasteye-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> The UAE government commended the confession from Saudi Arabia regarding the case. <sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Flag_of_Yemen.svg/23px-Flag_of_Yemen.svg.png" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Flag_of_Yemen.svg/45px-Flag_of_Yemen.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="450" data-file-height="300" />&#160;</span>Yemen: President <a href="/wiki/Abdrabbuh_Mansur_Hadi" title="Abdrabbuh Mansur Hadi">Abdrabbuh Mansur Hadi</a>, who has been living in exile in Saudi Arabia since 2015, said that "The cheap political and media targeting of Saudi Arabia will not deter it from continuing its leading role in the Arab and Islamic worlds."<sup id="cite_ref-middleeasteye_136-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-middleeasteye-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Asia">Asia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Killing_of_Jamal_Khashoggi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Asia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<ul><li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9f/Flag_of_Indonesia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Indonesia.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9f/Flag_of_Indonesia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Indonesia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9f/Flag_of_Indonesia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Indonesia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="450" data-file-height="300" />&#160;</span>Indonesia: President, <a href="/wiki/Joko_Widodo" title="Joko Widodo">Joko Widodo</a> said he was "deeply concerned" about the killing of Khashoggi and that he wanted a transparent investigation. Widodo met with Saudi Foreign Minister <a href="/wiki/Adel_al-Jubeir" title="Adel al-Jubeir">Adel al-Jubeir</a> at the presidential palace in the <a href="/wiki/West_Java" title="West Java">West Java</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Bogor" title="Bogor">Bogor</a>. Widodo\'s concerns were relayed by Indonesia\'s foreign minister following the meeting. The minister, <a href="/wiki/Retno_Marsudi" title="Retno Marsudi">Retno Marsudi</a>, told reporters that "the president is deeply concerned with the Khashoggi case and Indonesia hopes that the ongoing investigation will be transparent and meticulous."<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9e/Flag_of_Japan.svg/23px-Flag_of_Japan.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9e/Flag_of_Japan.svg/35px-Flag_of_Japan.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9e/Flag_of_Japan.svg/45px-Flag_of_Japan.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>Japan: Chief Cabinet Secretary <a href="/wiki/Yoshihide_Suga" title="Yoshihide Suga">Yoshihide Suga</a> told a press conference that the death of Jamal Khashoggi is "extremely regretful", according to Japanese news agency <a href="/wiki/Kyodo" class="mw-redirect" title="Kyodo">Kyodo</a>. Suga stated that Japan "strongly hopes for an early discovery of the truth and fair, transparent responses" through Turkey\'s investigation of the case.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPJPN_124-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPJPN-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Oceania">Oceania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Killing_of_Jamal_Khashoggi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Oceania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<ul><li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/46px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="640" />&#160;</span>Australia: Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Scott_Morrison" title="Scott Morrison">Scott Morrison</a> has condemned the death of Khashoggi, but announced it was no longer \xe2\x80\x9cappropriate\xe2\x80\x9d to attend next week\xe2\x80\x99s Future Investment Initiative in Riyadh. \xe2\x80\x9cWe deplore the killing of Jamal Khashoggi. We expect the Saudi government to cooperate fully with Turkish authorities regarding the investigation of this matter. Australia will stand with all other like-minded countries in condemning this death, this killing, and we expect there to be full cooperation. Those who have been arrested will go through the proper process. And we expect the truth to be determined through that process and those responsible to be held accountable,\xe2\x80\x9d Morrison said.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Commercial_interests">Commercial interests</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Killing_of_Jamal_Khashoggi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Commercial interests">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Richard_Branson" title="Richard Branson">Richard Branson</a> issued a statement on 11 October that he was suspending his advisory role for the two <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Vision_2030" title="Saudi Vision 2030">Saudi Vision 2030</a>-related projects amidst the Khashoggi controversy.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> \n</p><p><a href="/wiki/JPMorgan_Chase" title="JPMorgan Chase">JPMorgan Chase</a> CEO <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Dimon" title="Jamie Dimon">Jamie Dimon</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-reuters1_144-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-reuters1-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/BlackRock" title="BlackRock">BlackRock</a> CEO <a href="/wiki/Laurence_D._Fink" title="Laurence D. Fink">Larry Fink</a>, <a href="/wiki/The_Blackstone_Group" title="The Blackstone Group">The Blackstone Group</a> CEO <a href="/wiki/Stephen_A._Schwarzman" title="Stephen A. Schwarzman"> Stephen Schwarzman</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-FIIcnn_145-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIIcnn-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a> Cloud Chief Executive <a href="/wiki/Diane_Greene" title="Diane Greene">Diane Greene</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Viacom" title="Viacom">Viacom</a> CEO <a href="/wiki/Robert_Bakish" title="Robert Bakish">Robert Bakish</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uber" title="Uber">Uber</a> CEO <a href="/wiki/Dara_Khosrowshahi" title="Dara Khosrowshahi">Dara Khosrowshahi</a>, <a href="/wiki/AOL" title="AOL">AOL</a> co-founder <a href="/wiki/Steve_Case" title="Steve Case">Steve Case</a>, Richard Branson\'s <a href="/wiki/Virgin_Group" title="Virgin Group">Virgin Group</a>, <a href="/wiki/World_Bank" title="World Bank">World Bank</a> President <a href="/wiki/Jim_Yong_Kim" title="Jim Yong Kim">Jim Yong Kim</a>, the <i><a href="/wiki/Financial_Times" title="Financial Times">Financial Times</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Bloomberg_L.P." title="Bloomberg L.P.">Bloomberg</a>, <a href="/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">CNN</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Economist" title="The Economist">The Economist</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/CNBC" title="CNBC">CNBC</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ford_Motor" class="mw-redirect" title="Ford Motor">Ford Motor</a> chairman <a href="/wiki/Bill_Ford" class="mw-redirect" title="Bill Ford">Bill Ford</a> all withdrew their participation in the Saudi <a href="/wiki/Future_Investment_Initiative" title="Future Investment Initiative">Future Investment Initiative</a> (FII), which is in its second year.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Y_Combinator" title="Y Combinator">Y Combinator</a> CEO <a href="/wiki/Sam_Altman" title="Sam Altman">Sam Altman</a> announced that he is suspending his "involvement with the <a href="/wiki/NEOM" class="mw-redirect" title="NEOM">NEOM</a> advisory board until the facts regarding Jamal Khashoggi\xe2\x80\x99s disappearance are known".<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Siemens" title="Siemens">Siemens</a> CEO <a href="/wiki/Joe_Kaeser" title="Joe Kaeser">Joe Kaeser</a> pulled out the day before conference start.<sup id="cite_ref-reutersSim_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-reutersSim-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/French_Ministry_for_the_Economy_and_Finance" title="French Ministry for the Economy and Finance">French finance minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Bruno_Le_Maire" title="Bruno Le Maire">Bruno Le Maire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Finance_(Netherlands)" title="Ministry of Finance (Netherlands)">Dutch finance minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Wopke_Hoekstra" title="Wopke Hoekstra">Wopke Hoekstra</a>, British <a href="/wiki/Secretary_of_State_for_International_Trade" title="Secretary of State for International Trade">Secretary of State for International Trade</a> <a href="/wiki/Liam_Fox" title="Liam Fox">Liam Fox</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_the_Treasury" title="United States Secretary of the Treasury">United States Secretary of the Treasury</a> <a href="/wiki/Steven_Mnuchin" title="Steven Mnuchin">Steven Mnuchin</a>, <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> Managing Director <a href="/wiki/Christine_Lagarde" title="Christine Lagarde">Christine Lagarde</a> withdrew their participation in the FII conference as well.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Canada" title="Government of Canada">Government of Canada</a> has also indicated that they have no intention of sending anyone to the conference.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Bahrain\'s foreign minister <a href="/wiki/Khalid_bin_Ahmed_Al_Khalifa" title="Khalid bin Ahmed Al Khalifa">Khalid bin Ahmed Al Khalifa</a> called for a boycott of <a href="/wiki/Uber" title="Uber">Uber</a> in Bahrain and Saudi Arabia,<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> urging to "boycott anyone who boycotts Saudi Arabia". The <a href="/wiki/Public_Investment_Fund_of_Saudi_Arabia" title="Public Investment Fund of Saudi Arabia">Public Investment Fund of Saudi Arabia</a> invested $3.5 billion in Uber in 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-reuters1_144-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-reuters1-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Four American senators, including two members of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate_Committee_on_Foreign_Relations" title="United States Senate Committee on Foreign Relations">Committee on Foreign Relations</a>, urged <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling" title="Professional wrestling">professional wrestling</a> company <a href="/wiki/WWE" title="WWE">WWE</a> (which involves sitting <a href="/wiki/Administrator_of_the_Small_Business_Administration" title="Administrator of the Small Business Administration">Administrator of the Small Business Administration</a> <a href="/wiki/Linda_McMahon" title="Linda McMahon">Linda McMahon</a>) to reconsider its business relationship with Saudi Arabia, particularly its upcoming event, <a href="/wiki/WWE_Crown_Jewel" title="WWE Crown Jewel">Crown Jewel</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Knox_County,_Tennessee" title="Knox County, Tennessee">Knox County</a> Mayor <a href="/wiki/Kane_(wrestler)" title="Kane (wrestler)">Glenn Jacobs</a>, who wrestles for WWE under the ring name Kane, is scheduled to take part in the show. His spokesman said, "Mayor Jacobs won\'t speculate on Mr. Khashoggi\'s disappearance. However, he and his family are in the mayor\'s thoughts and prayers."<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup> The on-sale ticket date for Crown Jewel (previously 19 October) was removed from WWE.com, and no venue is specified.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>On 18 October, Twitter suspended a number of suspected <a href="/wiki/Twitter_bot" title="Twitter bot">bot accounts</a> constructed to support Mohammed bin Salman, and appearing to smear Khashoggi.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline"
